    [OfferPrice] decimal(14,2) NOT NULL,
    [IsAccepted] bit NOT NULL,
    [ProductId] int NOT NULL,
    [AppUserId] int NOT NULL,
    [CreatedDate] datetime2 NOT NULL,
    [LastModifiedDate] datetime2 NULL,
    CONSTRAINT [PK_Offers] PRIMARY KEY ([Id]),
    CONSTRAINT [FK_Offers_AspNetUsers_AppUserId] FOREIGN KEY ([AppUserId]) REFERENCES [AspNetUsers] ([Id]) ON DELETE CASCADE,
    CONSTRAINT [FK_Offers_Products_ProductId] FOREIGN KEY ([ProductId]) REFERENCES [Products] ([Id]) ON DELETE NO ACTION
);

INNER JOIN [Brands] AS [b] ON [t].[BrandId] = [b].[Id]
LEFT JOIN (
    SELECT [p0].[ProductImageFilesId], [p0].[ProductsId], [t1].[Id], [t1].[CreatedDate], [t1].[Discriminator], [t1].[FileName], [t1].[LastModifiedDate], [t1].[Path], [t1].[Storage], [t1].[Showcase]
    FROM [ProductProductImageFile] AS [p0]
    INNER JOIN (
        SELECT [b0].[Id], [b0].[CreatedDate], [b0].[Discriminator], [b0].[FileName], [b0].[LastModifiedDate], [b0].[Path], [b0].[Storage], [b0].[Showcase]
        FROM [BaseFiles] AS [b0]
        WHERE [b0].[Discriminator] = N'ProductImageFile'
    ) AS [t1] ON [p0].[ProductImageFilesId] = [t1].[Id]
) AS [t0] ON [t].[Id] = [t0].[ProductsId]
ORDER BY [t].[Id], [b].[Id], [t0].[ProductImageFilesId], [t0].[ProductsId]
